## Idea

Transpositions are permutations that swap two elements.

## Definitions

### Transpositions

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5417" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5424" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#5424" class="Module">_</a>

### Any transposition on a type equipped with a counting is a standard transposition

      <a id="19942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19943" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2290" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="19963" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19964" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="19968" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12852" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="19970" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#19907" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19971" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19974" class="Symbol">→</a>

        <a id="23928" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23929" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6142" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="23958" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12835" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="23961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23962" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="23966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23967" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23971" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13266" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="23997" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24000" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23773" class="Bound">x</a><a id="24001" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="24088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24089" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6142" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="24118" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12835" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="24121" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24122" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="24126" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24127" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="24131" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13266" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="24157" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24160" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23775" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24161" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Transpositions can be transported along equivalences

        <a id="29919" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29921" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29923" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>

          <a id="29999" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30001" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29176" class="Function">correct-transposition-conjugation-equiv-list</a> <a id="30046" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29737" class="Bound">li</a> <a id="30049" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29741" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30050" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30053" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
          <a id="30065" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30067" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>
            <a id="30082" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30084" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30086" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30086" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="30088" class="Symbol">→</a>
              <a id="30104" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a>
                <a id="30130" class="Symbol">((((</a><a id="30134" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24292" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="30136" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30139" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8449" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="30153" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29735" class="Bound">t</a><a id="30154" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30156" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30159" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30086" class="Bound">g</a><a id="30160" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30162" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30165" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#11010" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a> <a id="30197" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29737" class="Bound">li</a><a id="30199" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30201" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30204" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="30214" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24292" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30215" class="Symbol">)</a>
                <a id="30233" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30235" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29741" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30236" class="Symbol">))</a>
            <a id="30251" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30253" href="foundation.equivalences.html#15194" class="Function">left-inverse-law-equiv</a> <a id="30276" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24292" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30277" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### For all `n : ℕ`, for each transposition of `Fin n`, there exists a matching transposition in `Fin (succ-ℕ n)`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-succ-Fin-transposition"></a><a id="30410" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30410" class="Function">Fin-succ-Fin-transposition</a> <a id="30437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30440" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30440" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="30442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30444" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="30445" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30447" class="Symbol">→</a> 
  <a id="30452" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30454" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a>

    <a id="30496" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30498" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30500" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30500" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30502" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30504" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4972" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30520" class="Number">2</a> <a id="30522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30523" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="30525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30526" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="30530" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30440" class="Bound">n</a><a id="30531" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30533" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30536" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30536" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30538" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30540" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2290" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="30560" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30561" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30500" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30563" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30536" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30564" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="30570" class="Symbol">→</a> 
    <a id="30577" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30579" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a>

      <a id="30634" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30636" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30638" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30638" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30640" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="30650" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4972" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30666" class="Number">2</a>
          <a id="30678" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30680" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="30682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30683" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="30687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30688" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="30695" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30440" class="Bound">n</a><a id="30696" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30699" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30702" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30702" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30704" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30706" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2290" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="30726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30727" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30638" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30729" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30702" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30730" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

  <a id="39729" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#39321" class="Function">g</a> <a id="39731" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#39731" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="39733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39734" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1276" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="39738" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#39738" class="Bound">p</a><a id="39739" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39741" class="Symbol">=</a>

      <a id="39757" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="39759" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="39761" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a>
